<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>1.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt"><B>Nature of 
operations </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:3%; font-size:11pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The condensed interim consolidated 
financial statements of Turquoise Hill Resources Ltd. (&#147;Turquoise 
Hill&#148;) were
authorized for issue in accordance with a directors&#146; resolution on August 
2, 2016.&nbsp;Rio Tinto plc is the ultimate parent company and indirectly owns a
50.8% majority interest in Turquoise Hill as at June 30, 2016. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:3%; font-size:11pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">Turquoise Hill, together with its 
subsidiaries (collectively referred to as &#147;the Company&#148;), is an 
international
mining company focused principally on the operation and further development of 
the Oyu Tolgoi copper-gold mine in Southern Mongolia.&nbsp;Turquoise Hill&#146;s
head office is located at 354-200 Granville Street, Vancouver, British Columbia,
Canada,
V6C 1S4.&nbsp;Turquoise Hill&#146;s registered office is located at 300-204 
Black Street, Whitehorse, Yukon, Canada, Y1A 2M9. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:3%; font-size:11pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">Turquoise Hill has its primary 
listing in Canada on the Toronto Stock Exchange and secondary listings in the 
U.S. on the New
York Stock Exchange and the NASDAQ. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-
top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>2.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt"><B>Summary of 
significant accounting policies </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>(a)</I></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt"><I>Statement of 
compliance </I></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:11pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">These condensed interim 
consolidated financial statements have been prepared in accordance with 
International Financial
Reporting Standards (&#147;IFRS&#148;) as issued by the International Accounting
Standards Board (&#147;IASB&#148;) applicable to the preparation of interim 
financial statements, including IAS 34, <I>Interim Financial Reporting
</I>(&#147;IAS&nbsp;34&#148;).&nbsp;These condensed interim consolidated 
financial statements are compliant with IAS 34 and do not include all of the 
information required for full annual financial statements. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:11pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">These condensed interim 
consolidated financial statements should be read in conjunction with the 
Company&#146;s annual
financial statements for the year ended December 31, 2015, prepared in 
accordance with IFRS. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-
bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>(b)</I></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt"><I>New standards
and interpretations not yet adopted </I></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:11pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">A number of new standards, and 
amendments to standards and interpretations, are not yet effective for the year 
ending December
31, 2016, and have not been applied in preparing these condensed interim 
consolidated financial statements.&nbsp;The following standards may have a 
potential effect on the condensed interim consolidated financial statements of 
the Company: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>(i)</I></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ;
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt"><I></I>IFRS 9, 
<I>Financial Instruments</I>, is mandatorily effective for the Company&#146;s 
condensed interim
consolidated financial statements for the year ending December 31, 
2018.&nbsp;IFRS 9 brings together the classification and measurement, impairment
and hedge accounting phases of the IASB&#146;s project to replace IAS 39, 
<I>Financial Instruments:
Recognition and Measurement</I>. IFRS 9 retains but simplifies the mixed 
measurement model and establishes three primary measurement categories for 
financial assets: amortized cost; fair value through profit and loss; and fair 
value through other
comprehensive income. IFRS 9 also amends some of the requirements of IFRS 7, 
<I>Financial Instruments: Disclosures</I>, including added disclosures about 
investments in equity instruments measured at fair value in other comprehensive 
income, and
guidance on financial liabilities and derecognition of financial 
instruments.&nbsp;The extent of the impact of adoption has not yet been 
determined. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="center">7 </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times

<P STYLE="line-height:1.5pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ;

<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>(b)</I></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt"><I>New standards
and interpretations not yet adopted (continued) </I></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>(ii)</I></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt"><I></I>IFRS 15, 
<I>Revenue from Contracts with Customers</I>, which will replace IAS 18, 
<I>Revenue</I>, is
effective for the Company&#146;s fiscal year ending December 31, 2018 and is 
available for early adoption.&nbsp;The standard contains a single model that 
applies to contracts with customers.&nbsp;Revenue is recognized as control is 
passed to the
customer, either at a point in time or over time.&nbsp;New estimates and 
judgmental thresholds have been introduced, which may affect the amount and/or 
timing of revenue recognized.&nbsp;The extent of the impact of adoption of the 
standard has not
yet been determined. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-
top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>(iii)</I></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt"><I></I>IFRS 16, 
<I>Leases</I>, which will replace IAS 17, <I>Leases</I>, is effective for the 
Company&#146;s
fiscal year ending December 31, 2019 and is available for early 
adoption.&nbsp;The objective of the new standard is to report all leases on the 
consolidated statement of financial position and to define how leases and 
liabilities are
measured.&nbsp;The extent of the impact of adoption of the standard has not yet 
been determined. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman" 
ALIGN="justify">None
of the remaining standards and amendments to standards and interpretations are 
expected to have a significant effect on the consolidated financial statements 
of the Company. </P>

gold
concentrate sales to customers in China and revenue from individual customers in
excess of 10% of Oyu Tolgoi&#146;s revenue was $77.1 million, $71.3 million, 
$68.4 million and $66.9 million (June 30, 2015 - $100.3 million, $76.6 million
and $48.5
million) respectively.&nbsp;Revenue by geographic destination is based on the 
ultimate country of destination, if known.&nbsp;If the destination of the copper
concentrate sold through traders is not known, then revenue is allocated to the 
location
of the copper concentrate at the time when revenue is recognized.

respectively.&nbsp;Revenue by geographic destination is based on the ultimate 
country of destination, if known.&nbsp;If the destination of the copper 
concentrate sold through traders is not known, then revenue is allocated to the 
location of the
copper concentrate at the time when revenue is recognized.

syndicate of
international financial institutions and export credit agencies representing the
governments of Canada, the United States and Australia, along with 15 commercial
banks.</P>

<TD WIDTH="6%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(i)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt">The carrying 
value of the Company&#146;s borrowings differs from fair value due to amortized 
transaction
costs. At June&nbsp;30, 2016, borrowings are stated net of $216.2 million 
amortized transaction costs. Other than amortized transaction costs, at June 30,
2016 the fair value of the Company&#146;s borrowings approximates carrying value
since, other
than fixed interest amounts under the Export Credit Agencies facility, they 
carry floating rates of interest, and because of the relative proximity of 
drawdown to the reporting date. This is considered a level&nbsp;2 fair value 
measurement.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-
bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="6%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(ii)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt">The project 
finance facility provides for interest only payments for the first five years 
and is then
structured as a stepped amortization schedule for the remaining life of the 
facility. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-
bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="2%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>(b)</I></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt"><I>Revolving 
credit facility </I></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:6%; font-size:11pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">In March 2016, Oyu Tolgoi signed an
amendment to extend the existing secured $200.0 million revolving credit 
facility with
five banks that was scheduled to mature on March 19, 2016.&nbsp;Amounts under 
the credit facility were required to be used by Oyu Tolgoi for working capital 
purposes.&nbsp;The credit facility expired on draw down under the project 
finance facility
described in (a) above. </P>

<TR>
<TD WIDTH="2%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>(a)</I></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt"><I>Common share 
investments funded on behalf of non-controlling interests 
</I></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:6%; font-size:11pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">Since 2011, the Company has funded 
common share investments in Oyu Tolgoi on behalf of Erdenes Oyu Tolgoi LLC
(&#147;Erdenes&#148;). In accordance with the Amended and Restated Shareholders 
Agreement dated June 8, 2011, such funded amounts earn interest at an effective 
annual rate of LIBOR plus 6.5% and are repayable to the Company via a pledge 
over
Erdenes&#146; share of future Oyu Tolgoi common share dividends. Erdenes also 
has the right to reduce the outstanding balance by making payments directly to 
the Company. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:6%; font-size:11pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">Common share investments funded on 
behalf of Erdenes are recorded as a reduction to the net carrying value of non-
controlling
interest. As at June 30, 2016, the cumulative amount of such funding was $751.1 
million (December&nbsp;31, 2015 - $751.1 million). Accrued interest of $265.9 
million (December 31, 2015 - $231.1 million), has not been recognized in these 
condensed
interim consolidated financial statements, as payment will be triggered on 
common share dividend distribution by Oyu Tolgoi, the timing of which cannot 
currently be reliably determined. </P>

STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="center">20 </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:3%; font-size:11pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The basic earnings per share is 
computed by dividing the net income attributable to common stock by the weighted
average
number of common shares outstanding during the period.&nbsp;All stock options 
and share purchase warrants outstanding at each period end have been excluded 
from the weighted average share calculation. </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:16pt; font-family:Times

<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times

<P STYLE="line-height:1.5pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-

<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><B>23. Related parties (continued) </B></P>
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="2%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;(a)</I></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt"><I>Related party
transactions with Rio Tinto (continued) </I></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="6%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>(ii)</I></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt"><I></I>As part 
of project finance (Note 16), Turquoise Hill appointed 9539549 Canada Inc., a 
wholly owned
subsidiary of Rio Tinto, as service provider to provide post-drawdown cash 
management services in connection with net proceeds from the project finance 
facility, which shall be placed with 9539549 Canada Inc. and returned to 
Turquoise Hill as
required for purposes of funding the Oyu Tolgoi underground mine.&nbsp;Rio Tinto
International Holdings Limited, a wholly owned subsidiary of Rio Tinto, has 
guaranteed the obligations of the service provider under this agreement. At 
June&nbsp;30,
2016, amounts due from 9539549 Canada Inc. totalled $4,156.3 million, earning 
interest at an effective annual rate of LIBOR plus 2.45%.&nbsp;The interest rate
reflects: interest receivable at LIBOR minus 0.05%; and a benefit of 2.5% 
arising on
amounts deposited with 9539549 Canada Inc. under the cash management services 
agreement, which are net settled with the 2.5% completion support fee described 
in (v) below. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="6%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>(iii)</I></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ;
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt"><I></I>In 
accordance with the Amended and Restated Shareholders Agreement, which was 
signed on June 8, 2011,
and other related agreements, Turquoise Hill is required to pay a management 
services payment to Rio Tinto equal to a percentage of all capital costs and 
operating costs incurred by Oyu Tolgoi from March 31, 2010 onwards. Until the 
Oyu Tolgoi open
pit mine achieved Commencement of Production, as defined in the Investment 
Agreement, on September&nbsp;1, 2013, the percentage of costs used to calculate 
the management services payment was 1.5%.&nbsp;Thereafter, the percentage 
increased to 3.0%
for open pit operations and, in accordance with the Oyu Tolgoi Underground Mine 
Development and Financing Plan (&#147;UDP&#148;) signed on May&nbsp;18, 2015, is
1.5% for Underground capital costs. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="6%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>(iv)</I></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt"><I></I>Rio Tinto
recovers the costs of providing general corporate support services and mine 
management
services to Turquoise Hill. Mine management services are provided by Rio Tinto 
in its capacity as the manager of the Oyu Tolgoi mine. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TR>
<TD WIDTH="6%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>(v)</I></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt"><I></I>As part 
of the project finance agreements (Note 16), Rio Tinto provided a guarantee, 
known as the
completion support undertaking (&#147;CSU&#148;) in favour of the Commercial 
Banks and the Export Credit Agencies. In consideration for providing the CSU, 
Oyu Tolgoi and Turquoise Hill are required to pay Rio Tinto a fee equal to 2.5% 
of the amounts
drawn under the facility, of which 1.9% is payable by Oyu Tolgoi and 0.6% is 
payable by Turquoise Hill. The annual completion support fee of 2.5% on amounts 
drawn under the facility is accounted for as a borrowing cost and included 
within interest
expense and similar charges (refer to Note&nbsp;8). The fee is settled net of a 
benefit arising on amounts deposited with 9539549 Canada Inc. under the cash 
management services agreement described in (ii) above. The fee payment 
obligation will
terminate on the date Rio Tinto&#146;s CSU obligations to the project lenders 
terminate. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
margin-left:2%; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The
above
noted transactions were carried out in the normal course of operations and were 
measured at the transaction amount, which is the amount of consideration 
established and agreed to by the related parties. </P>

measured at the transaction amount, which is the amount of consideration 
established and agreed to by the related parties. </P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New 
Roman"><B>24.&nbsp;Contingencies
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:3%; font-
size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">Due to the size, 
complexity and nature of Turquoise Hill&#146;s operations, various legal and tax
matters arise in
the ordinary course of business. Turquoise Hill recognizes a liability with 
respect to such matters when an outflow of economic resources is assessed as 
probable and the amount can be reliably estimated.&nbsp;In the opinion of 
management, these
matters will not have a material effect on the condensed interim consolidated 
financial statements of the Company. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>25.&nbsp;Financial 
instruments and
fair value measurements </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
margin-left:3%; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman" 
ALIGN="justify">Certain of the Company&#146;s financial assets and liabilities 
are measured at fair value on
a recurring basis and classified in their entirety based on the lowest level of 
input that is significant to the fair value measurement. Certain non-financial 
assets and liabilities may also be measured at fair value on a non-recurring 
basis. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:3%; font-size:11pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The fair value of financial assets 
and financial liabilities measured at amortized cost is determined in accordance
with
accepted pricing models based on discounted cash flow analysis or using prices 
from observable current market transactions.&nbsp;Except as otherwise specified,
the Company considers that the carrying amount of trade and other receivables, 
trade
payables and other financial assets measured at amortized cost approximates 
their fair value because of the demand nature or short-term maturity of these 
instruments. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:3%; font-size:11pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The following tables provide an 
analysis of the Company&#146;s financial assets that are measured subsequent to 
initial
recognition at fair value on a recurring basis, grouped into Level 1 to 3 based 
on the degree to which the inputs used to determine the fair value are 
observable. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-
bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#9679;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt">Level 1 fair 
value measurements are those derived from quoted prices in active markets for 
identical assets or
liabilities. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt">Level 2 fair 
value measurements are those derived from inputs other than quoted prices 
included within
Level&nbsp;1, that are observable either directly or indirectly. 
</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:11pt">Level 3 fair 
value measurements are those derived from valuation techniques that include 
inputs that are not
based on observable market data.</P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:ARIAL"><B>Turquoise Hill Resources Ltd. </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-
family:ARIAL">Management&#146;s Discussion and Analysis of Financial Condition 
and Results of Operations </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:7pt; font-
family:ARIAL">(Stated in U.S. dollars, except where noted) </P> <P STYLE="line-
height:1.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1.00pt solid 
#000000">&nbsp;</P>
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" 
BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>1.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><B>OVERVIEW 
</B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify"><B>Financial Results and Review of Operations for the Second 
Quarter 2016 </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:8pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-
bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" 
BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Oyu Tolgoi achieved an 
excellent safety performance with an All Injury Frequency Rate of 0.13 per 
200,000 hours worked
for the six months ended June 30, 2016. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-
size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" 
BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ;
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">On May 5, 2016, Oyu Tolgoi
received the formal notice to proceed for underground development by the boards 
of Turquoise
Hill, Rio Tinto and Oyu Tolgoi LLC. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-
size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" 
BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">As part of the notice to 
proceed process, the 2016 Oyu Tolgoi Feasibility Study was approved. 
</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" 
BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">In June 2016, Oyu Tolgoi 
signed a critical contract with Jacobs Engineering Group to provide engineering,
procurement
and construction management services for underground development. 
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-
bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" 
BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Major contractor 
mobilization for the sinking of Shafts #2 and #5, underground development, 
critical construction works
and maintenance are all progressing. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-
size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" 
BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">As of June 30, 2016, Oyu 
Tolgoi had drawn down approximately $4.3 billion of the project finance facility
and used all
net proceeds to pay down shareholder loans payable to Turquoise Hill. 
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:8pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-
bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" 
BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Turquoise Hill deposited 
net project finance funds of approximately $4.2 billion with Rio Tinto in 
Q2&#146;16.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:8pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-
bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" 
BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Oyu Tolgoi recorded 
revenue of $329.7 million in Q2&#146;16, a decrease of 22.0% over Q1&#146;16, 
reflecting mainly
lower gold sales volumes. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-
top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" 
BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Turquoise Hill generated 
operating cash flow before interest and taxes of $161.6 million during 
Q2&#146;16.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-
bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" 
BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">For Q2&#146;16, Turquoise 
Hill reported income from continuing operations attributable to shareholders of 
$29.8 million.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-
bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" 
BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">In Q2&#146;16, 
concentrator throughput was broadly consistent with Q1&#146;16; resulting in 
average throughput of
approximately 105,000 tonnes per day for the quarter. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P 
STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" 
BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Copper production in 
Q2&#146;16 declined 10.3% over Q1&#146;16 reflecting lower grades from reduced 
mining in Phase 2
and relative lower recovery from Phase 6 ore. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P 
STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" 
BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">As expected, gold 
production in Q2&#146;16 declined approximately 52% over Q1&#146;16, due to 
lower grades from reduced
mining in Phase 2. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-
top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"
BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Concentrate volumes sold 
in Q2&#146;16 increased 6.7% over Q1&#146;16. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"

<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">For Q2&#146;16, Oyu

pound of copper. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-
top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-

<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:ARIAL"><B>Turquoise Hill Resources Ltd. </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-
family:ARIAL">Management&#146;s Discussion and Analysis of Financial Condition 
and Results of Operations </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:7pt; font-
family:ARIAL">(Stated in U.S. dollars, except where noted) </P> <P STYLE="line-
height:1.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1.00pt solid 
#000000">&nbsp;</P>
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:ARIAL"><B>3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;REVIEW OF OPERATIONS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify">Turquoise Hill is an international mining company focused on the
operation and further development of the Oyu Tolgoi copper-gold mine in southern
Mongolia, which is the Company&#146;s principal material mineral resource 
property. The Oyu Tolgoi mine is held through a 66% interest in Oyu Tolgoi LLC 
(Oyu Tolgoi); the remaining 34% interest is held by Erdenes Oyu Tolgoi LLC 
(Erdenes). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify">In Q2&#146;16, the Company recorded net income attributable to 
owners of Turquoise Hill of $29.8 million ($0.01 per share) compared with net
income of
$24.9 million ($0.01 per share) in Q2&#146;15, an increase of $4.9 million.</P> 
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify">Operating cash flows before interest and taxes in Q2&#146;16 
were $161.6
million compared with $239.2 million in Q2&#146;15, reflecting the impact of 
reduced gold production and sales in concentrates. </P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify">Capital expenditure
on property, plant and equipment was $53.3 million on a cash basis in 
Q2&#146;16, attributed to both underground pre-start and sustaining capital 
activities. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify">Turquoise Hill&#146;s cash and cash equivalents at June 30, 2016
were approximately $1.5 billion. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:ARIAL"><B>A.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;OYU TOLGOI </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify">The Oyu Tolgoi mine is
approximately 550 kilometres south of Ulaanbaatar, Mongolia&#146;s capital city,
and 80 kilometres north of the Mongolia-China border. Mineralization on the 
property consists of porphyry-style copper, gold, silver and molybdenum 
contained in a
linear structural trend (the Oyu Tolgoi Trend) that has a strike length 
extending over 26 kilometres. Mineral resources have been identified in a series
of deposits throughout this trend. They include, from south to north, the Heruga
Deposit, the
Southern Oyu deposits (Southwest Oyu, South Oyu, Wedge and Central Oyu) and the 
Hugo Dummett deposits (Hugo South, Hugo North and Hugo North Extension). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify">The Oyu Tolgoi mine has initially been developed as an open-pit 
operation. A copper concentrator plant, with related facilities and necessary
infrastructure to support a nominal throughput of 100,000 tonnes of ore per day,
has been constructed to process ore mined from the Southern Oyu open pit. Long-
term development plans for Oyu Tolgoi are based on a 95,000-tonne-per-day 
underground
block-cave mine. In August 2013, development of the underground mine was 
suspended pending resolution of matters with the Government of Mongolia. 
Following signing of the Oyu Tolgoi Underground Mine Development and Financing 
Plan (Underground Plan)
in May 2015 and the signing of a $4.4 billion project finance facility in 
December 2015, Oyu Tolgoi received the formal notice to proceed approval by the 
boards of Turquoise Hill, Rio Tinto and Oyu Tolgoi LLC on May 5, 2016. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:ARIAL"><B>Preparation for underground development </B></P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify">Prior to suspending
underground construction in August 2013, underground lateral development at Hugo
North Lift 1 had advanced approximately 16 kilometres off Shaft #1. 
Approximately 65 kilometres of lateral development is expected to be complete by
the first draw
bell. A total of approximately 200 kilometres of lateral development are planned
over the life of Hugo North Lift 1. The following table outlines the shafts 
planned for underground development. </P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Following the approval of the Underground Plan in 
May 2015 and the filing of the revised schedules for the statutory
feasibility study with the Mongolian Minerals Council in August 2015, pre-start 
activities began. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Pre-start</FONT> activities 
included ramp-up of the owners&#146; and engineering, procurement and 
construction
management (EPCM) teams, detailed engineering and procurement for equipment and 
materials required for necessary critical works that are key enablers for 
recommencement of underground&nbsp;development mining activity. In June 2016, 
Oyu Tolgoi signed
a critical contract with Jacobs Engineering Group to provide EPCM services for 
underground development. Major contractor mobilization for the sinking for 
Shafts #2 and #5, underground development, critical construction works and 
maintenance are all
progressing. A site infrastructure office has been established as well as 
project personnel being mobilized. In July 2016, Oyu Tolgoi signed a contract 
with mining services provider Thiess and Mongolian contractor Khishig Arvin for 
development of
twin declines, incorporating both a service and a conveyor tunnel. </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:ARIAL"><B>Turquoise Hill Resources Ltd. </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-
family:ARIAL">Management&#146;s Discussion and Analysis of Financial Condition 
and Results of Operations </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:7pt; font-
family:ARIAL">(Stated in U.S. dollars, except where noted) </P> <P STYLE="line-
height:1.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1.00pt solid 
#000000">&nbsp;</P>
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:ARIAL"><B>Project finance and funding of Oyu Tolgoi by Turquoise Hill 
</B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify">In December 2015, Oyu Tolgoi signed a $4.4 billion project 
finance facility for underground development provided by a syndicate of 
international
financial institutions, export credit agencies representing the governments of 
Canada, the United States and Australia and 15 commercial banks. As of 
June&nbsp;30, 2016, Oyu Tolgoi had drawn down approximately $4.3 billion of the 
project finance
facility. Since the December 2015 signing, Oyu Tolgoi has used cash reserves to 
pay bank fees of approximately $0.2 billion. Steps are being taken to finalize 
the drawdown of the remaining amount. As part of the project finance facility, a
debt cap
of $6.0 billion for Oyu Tolgoi was agreed, which provides the possibility for an
additional $1.6 billion of supplemental debt in the future. </P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify">Net
funding received by Oyu Tolgoi of approximately $4.3 billion was used to pay 
down shareholder loans payable to the Company. Oyu Tolgoi&#146;s proceeds from 
project finance funds were reduced by bank fees and withholding taxes of 
approximately $0.1
billion in line with contractual obligations. Approximately $4.2 billion was 
placed on deposit with Rio Tinto, in accordance with the cash management 
services agreement (Cash Management Services Agreement). The amount on deposit 
with Rio Tinto will
be available for drawdown by Oyu Tolgoi as required for the development of the 
underground mine. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-
size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">In accordance with the Amended and
Restated
Shareholders&#146; Agreement (ARSHA) dated June&nbsp;8, 2011, Turquoise Hill has
funded Oyu Tolgoi&#146;s cash requirements beyond internally generated cash 
flows by a combination of equity investment and shareholder debt. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify">For amounts funded by debt, Oyu Tolgoi must repay such amounts, 
including accrued interest, before it can pay common share dividends. At 
June&nbsp;30,
2016 after the project finance drawdown, the aggregate outstanding balance of 
shareholder loans extended by subsidiaries of the Company to Oyu Tolgoi was $2.8
billion, including accrued interest of $0.5 million. These loans bear interest 
at an
effective annual rate of LIBOR plus 6.5%. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">In accordance 
with the ARSHA, a subsidiary of the Company has funded the common share 
investments in Oyu
Tolgoi on behalf of Erdenes. These funded amounts earn interest at an effective 
annual rate of LIBOR plus 6.5% and are repayable, by Erdenes to a subsidiary of 
the Company, via a pledge over Erdenes&#146; share of Oyu Tolgoi common share 
dividends.
Erdenes also has the right to reduce the outstanding balance by making cash 
payments at any time. As of June&nbsp;30, 2016, the cumulative amount of such 
funding was $751.1 million, representing 34% of invested common share equity; 
unrecognized
interest on the funding amounted to $265.9 million. </P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Feasibility 
study completion </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify">The 2016 Oyu Tolgoi Feasibility Study (2016 Feasibility Study) 
was approved in May 2016. The 2016 Feasibility Study is based on Oyu Tolgoi 
reserves. The
2016 Reserve Case includes mineral reserves from the Southern Oyu Tolgoi open 
pit and the Hugo North Lift&nbsp;1 block cave. Turquoise Hill expects to publish
an updated National Instrument 43-101 compliant independent technical report 
relating to
the project in the second half of 2016. </P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>

<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:ARIAL"><B>Turquoise Hill Resources Ltd. </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-
family:ARIAL">Management&#146;s Discussion and Analysis of Financial Condition 
and Results of Operations </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:7pt; font-
family:ARIAL">(Stated in U.S. dollars, except where noted) </P> <P STYLE="line-
height:1.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1.00pt solid 
#000000">&nbsp;</P>
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"
ALIGN="justify">Highlights of the 2016 Feasibility Study are as follows. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:8pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" 
BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:'WINGDINGS 2'">&#161;</FONT></FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">After-tax internal rate of
return of 18% (NPV<SUB STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:bottom">8%</SUB> of 
$4.6 billion)
assuming long-term copper and gold prices of $2.86 per pound and $1,201 per 
ounce respectively. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" 
BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New
Roman"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:'WINGDINGS 2'">&#161;</FONT></FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">With the exception of 
depletion from ongoing operations, there have been no material changes to the 
mineral reserve and
resource estimates included in the 2014 Oyu Tolgoi Technical Report (&#147;2014 
Technical Report&#148;). </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" 
BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:'WINGDINGS 2'">&#161;</FONT></FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Nominal expansion capital 
of $5.3 billion ($5.1 billion 2016 real costs) for the underground project, 
which is broadly
in-line with the $4.9 billion estimate (2014 real costs) contained in the 2014 
Technical Report. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" 
BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Project assumes a five-
year construction period, first sustainable underground production around 2021 
and five to
seven-year ramp up period. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" 
BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

Production
from the first draw bell is expected in 2020. Underground operations are 
expected to begin with first sustainable production in 2021. </P> <P

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:ARIAL"><B>Q2&#146;16 performance </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Safety
continues to be a major focus throughout Oyu Tolgoi&#146;s operations and the 
mine&#146;s management is committed to reducing risk and injury. Oyu Tolgoi 
achieved an excellent safety performance with an All Injury Frequency Rate of 
0.13 per 200,000
hours worked for the six months ended June 30, 2016. </P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:7pt; font-
family:ARIAL">* Any financial information in this MD&amp;A should be reviewed in
consultation with the Company&#145;s unaudited condensed interim
consolidated financial statements. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; font-size:7pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">** Please refer to
Section 13 &#150; NON-GAAP MEASURES &#150; on page 15 of this MD&amp;A for 
reconciliation of
these metrics, including total operating cash costs, to the financial 
statements. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:7pt; 
font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">*** Operating cash costs, C1 and all-in 
sustaining unit costs for
the three months ended March 31, 2016 have been revised to correctly reflect the
change in inventory as reported in the Company&#146;s reconciliation of net 
income (loss) to net cash flow generated from operating activities. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify">Revenue of $329.7 million in Q2&#146;16 decreased 22% over 
Q1&#146;16 mainly reflecting significantly reduced sales of gold in concentrates
driven by
lower gold head grades. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-
size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Production and delivery costs 
include primarily the cash costs in inventory sold as well as allocated mine 
administration
costs. Depreciation and depletion includes the depreciation and depletion in 
inventory sold as well as any depreciation of assets used in the selling and 
delivery process, including the depreciation of capitalized production phase 
stripping costs.
Q2&#146;16 cost of sales were $237.1 million (Q2&#146;15: $225.7 million) 
reflecting higher unit cost of production due to lower feed grade and lower 
recovery. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify">Capital expenditure, on a cash basis, for Q2&#146;16 was $53.3 
million (Q2&#146;15: $35.1 million) including amounts attributed to both 
underground
(including pre-start) and sustaining activities of $36.5 million and $14.1 
million respectively. Sustaining capital expenditure includes the tailings 
storage facility and deferred stripping. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify">Total operating cash costs at Oyu Tolgoi in Q2&#146;16 were
$215.5 million. The 5% royalty payable to the Government of Mongolia is 
reflected as a cash
operating expense; deferred stripping costs are not included in operating cash 
costs. Oyu Tolgoi administrative costs were $49.5 million reflecting increased 
management service fees incurred as a result of project finance drawdown during 
the
quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Oyu Tolgoi&#146;s C1 costs in Q2&#146;16 were 
$1.12 per pound, compared with $0.06 per pound in Q1&#146;16. The increase was 
mainly due to
lower gold sales, combined with lower copper production reflecting lower grades 
from reduced mining in Phase 2, and relative lower recovery from Phase 6 ore. 
</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify">All-in sustaining costs in Q2&#146;16 were $1.55 per pound, 
compared with $0.66 per pound in Q1&#146;16. The increase was mainly due to 
lower gold
revenues and the impact of reduced copper production. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Oyu Tolgoi&#146;s second quarter production 
reflected reduced mining in Phase 2 of the open pit. In Q2&#146;16,
concentrator throughput was consistent with Q1&#146;16; resulting in average 
throughput of approximately 105,000 tonnes per day for the quarter. Copper 
production in Q2&#146;16 declined 10.3% over Q1&#146;16 reflecting lower grades 
from reduced
mining in Phase 2 and relative lower recovery from Phase 6 ore. As expected, 
gold production in Q2&#146;16 declined approximately 52% over Q1&#146;16, due to
lower grades from reduced mining in Phase 2. Concentrate sold in Q2&#146;16 
increased 6.7%
over Q1&#146;16. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-
size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Operational outlook </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify">Open pit cash-basis
capital expenditure (excluding underground expenditure) in 2016 is expected to 
be approximately $200 million, compared with previous guidance of approximately 
$300 million. The reduction primarily reflects lower capitalization of deferred 
stripping
following open-pit optimization to reduce waste. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Operating 
cash costs in 2016 are now expected to be approximately $840 million, compared 
to the
previous estimate of $800 million. The change reflects the impact of: deferred 
stripping reclassification as part of open-pit optimization and additional 
management service fees incurred in relation to project finance, offset by 
further cost
rationalization and lower royalties due to lower gold sales in the second half
of 2016. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Sales contracts have been signed for essentially 
all of Oyu
Tolgoi&#146;s expected 2016 concentrate production. </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-
family:ARIAL">Management&#146;s Discussion and Analysis of Financial Condition 
and Results of Operations </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:7pt; font-
family:ARIAL">(Stated in U.S. dollars, except where noted) </P> <P STYLE="line-
height:1.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1.00pt solid 
#000000">&nbsp;</P>
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:ARIAL"><B>B.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;CORPORATE ACTIVITIES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:ARIAL"><B>Election of directors </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">The 
nominees set forth in the
Company&#146;s management proxy circular dated March&nbsp;15, 2016 were elected 
as directors of Turquoise Hill at the Annual Meeting of Shareholders, which took
place on May&nbsp;3, 2016. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:ARIAL"><B>C.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;CORPORATE ADMINISTRATIVE EXPENSES 
</B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify"><B>Corporate administrative expenses. </B>Corporate 
administrative costs in Q2&#146;16 were $4.1 million, a decrease of $1.7 million
from Q2&#146;15,
mainly due to lower consulting costs. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:ARIAL"><B>4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;LIQUIDITY AND CAPITAL RESOURCES 
</B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify">As at June&nbsp;30, 2016, Turquoise Hill held consolidated cash 
and cash equivalents of approximately $1.5 billion, consolidated working capital
(inclusive of cash and cash equivalents) of $2.2 billion and an accumulated 
deficit of $4.3 billion. Loans due from a related party of $4.2 billion have 
been recorded during Q2&#146;16, following the deposit of net proceeds (after 
settlement of
withholding taxes and transaction costs) from project finance drawdown with a 
subsidiary of Rio Tinto in accordance with a cash management services agreement
signed on December&nbsp;15, 2015. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:ARIAL"><B>Cash flow </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt;
font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><B><I>Operating activities. 
</I></B>A total of
$161.6 million of cash was generated from operating activities before interest 
and tax in Q2&#146;16 compared with 195.4 million in Q1&#146;16, reflecting the 
impact of lower gold revenues. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify"><B><I>Investing activities. </I></B>Cash used in investing 
activities totalled $4,206.9 million in Q2&#146;16, compared with $51.7 million 
in Q1&#146;16.
Under the Cash Management Services Agreement entered into as part of project 
finance, deposits of $4,156.3 million were made, during Q2&#146;16, with 9539549
Canada Inc., a wholly owned subsidiary of Rio Tinto. Property, plant and 
equipment
purchases of $53.3 million related to both Oyu Tolgoi underground <FONT 
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-start</FONT> and sustaining activities (including
deferred stripping and construction of tailings storage facility). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify"><B><I>Financing activities.</I></B> Cash generated from 
financing activities totalled $4,122.1 million in Q2&#146;16, compared with cash
used in
financing activities of $6.7 million in Q1&#146;16. Net proceeds from the 
project finance facility of $4,274.3 million ($4,307.3 million before project 
finance fee deduction at source) were partly offset by the payment of $152.3 
million project
finance fees with Oyu Tolgoi cash. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Liquidity and capital 
resources </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify">As of December&nbsp;31, 2015, Oyu Tolgoi had signed a $4.4 
billion project finance facility for the purposes of developing the underground 
mine.
Following drawdown under the facility, Turquoise Hill has recorded approximately
$4.2 billion of loans receivable from Rio Tinto arising from net proceeds 
deposited in accordance with the Cash Management Services Agreement. Turquoise 
Hill intends to
re-draw these amounts as required in order to fund future development of the 
underground mine. Please refer to Section&nbsp;3.A &#150; OYU TOLGOI &#150; on 
page 6 and to Section 12 &#150; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">RELATED-
PARTY</FONT>
TRANSACTIONS &#150; on page 14 of this MD&amp;A. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">In March 
2016, Oyu Tolgoi signed an amendment to extend the secured $200.0 million 
revolving credit
facility with five banks that was scheduled to mature on March&nbsp;19, 2016. 
Amounts under the credit facility were required to be used by Oyu Tolgoi for 
working capital purposes. The credit facility expired on drawdown under the 
project finance
facility. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:ARIAL"><B>Turquoise Hill Resources Ltd. </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-
family:ARIAL">Management&#146;s Discussion and Analysis of Financial Condition 
and Results of Operations </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:7pt; font-
family:ARIAL">(Stated in U.S. dollars, except where noted) </P> <P STYLE="line-
height:1.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1.00pt solid 
#000000">&nbsp;</P>
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"
ALIGN="justify">Turquoise Hill&#146;s financial performance and its ability to 
advance its future operations and
development plans are heavily dependent on the availability of funding, base and
precious metal prices and foreign-exchange rates. Volatility in these markets 
continues to be high. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify">For further details on the Company&#146;s financing plans, 
please refer to Section 4 &#150; LIQUIDITY AND CAPITAL RESOURCES &#150; on page 
11 of this
MD&amp;A. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:ARIAL"><B>Copper market </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Commodity prices 
are a key
driver of Turquoise Hill&#146;s earnings. In early June, copper prices declined 
to a four-month low of $2.04 per pound as large deliveries of cathode into 
London Metal Exchange (LME) Asian warehouses negatively impacted sentiment. 
During June,
prices recovered to $2.17 per pound on the back of a weaker U.S. dollar and 
expectations that the United Kingdom (UK) would remain part of the European 
Union (EU). The UK&#146;s subsequent vote to leave the EU on June&nbsp;23 
resulted in higher
volatility. By mid-July, prices had recovered to a two-month high of $2.23 per 
pound, on the expectation that looser monetary policy will support prices.
Prices are likely to remain volatile in the near-term and will be impacted by 
subsequent policy
announcements. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt;
font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Spot treatment and refining charges (TC/RCs) 
have moved up to $100-108/10-10.8. The China Smelter Purchasing Team raised its 
copper
concentrate floor to $103/10.3 for Q3&#146;16, up from $85/8.5 in Q2&#146;16, 
reflecting ample concentrate supplies in the spot market. A sharp rise in LME 
Asian cathode stocks since early June has more than offset a decline in Shanghai
Futures
Exchange stocks to leave total visible stocks up approximately 23,000 tonnes by 
early July. Stocks remain balanced relative to demand. </P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify">Gold prices
rallied to a two-year high of $1,369 per ounce in early July, boosted by safe 
haven demand in the wake of uncertainty surrounding the UK leaving the EU and 
market expectations of looser monetary policy. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:ARIAL"><B>Exchange Rates </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Oyu Tolgoi&#146;s
sales are settled in U.S.
dollars, and a portion of its expenses are incurred in local currencies. Foreign
exchange fluctuations could have an effect on Turquoise Hill&#146;s operating 
margins; however in view of the proportion of locally incurred expenditures, 
such
fluctuations are not expected to have a significant impact on Turquoise 
Hill&#146;s financial performance. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>7.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;OFF-
BALANCE SHEET
ARRANGEMENTS </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-
size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">During the six months ended June 
30, 2016, Turquoise Hill was not a party to any off-balance-sheet arrangements 
that have, or are
reasonably likely to have, a current or future effect on the results of 
operations, financial condition, revenues or expenses, liquidity, capital 
expenditures or capital resources of the Company. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:ARIAL"><B>8.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;CONTRACTUAL OBLIGATIONS </B></P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify">As at June
30, 2016, there were no significant changes in Turquoise Hill&#146;s contractual
obligations and commercial commitments from those disclosed in its MD&amp;A for 
the year ended December 31, 2015. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-

these estimates require judgments about matters that are inherently uncertain.

</TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:8pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:7pt" 
BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(i)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:7pt">In addition to placing cash
and cash equivalents on deposit with banks or investing funds with other 
financial
institutions, Turquoise Hill may deposit cash and cash equivalents or invest 
funds with Rio Tinto in accordance with an agreed upon policy and strategy for 
the management of liquid resources. At June 30, 2016, cash equivalents deposited
with wholly
owned subsidiaries of Rio Tinto totalled $741.7 million, earning interest at 
rates equivalent to those offered by financial institutions. 
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-
bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:7pt" 
BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(ii)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:7pt">As part of project finance,
Turquoise Hill appointed 9539549 Canada Inc., a wholly owned subsidiary of Rio 
Tinto, as
service provider to provide post-drawdown cash management services in connection
with net proceeds from the project finance facility, which shall be placed with 
9539549 Canada Inc. and returned to Turquoise Hill as required for purposes of 
funding
the Oyu Tolgoi underground mine. Rio Tinto International Holdings Limited, a 
wholly owned subsidiary of Rio Tinto, agreed to guarantee the obligations of the
service provider under this agreement. At June 30, 2016, amounts due from 
9539549 Canada
Inc. totalled $4,156.3 million, earning interest at an effective annual rate of 
LIBOR plus 2.45%. The interest rate reflects: interest receivable at LIBOR minus
0.05%; and a benefit of 2.5% arising on amounts deposited with 9539549 Canada
Inc. under
the Cash Management Services Agreement, which&nbsp;are net settled with the 2.5%
completion support fee&nbsp;described in (v) below. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P 
STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:7pt" 
BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(iii)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:7pt">In accordance with the 
ARSHA, which was signed on June 8, 2011, and other related agreements, Turquoise
Hill is required
to pay a management services payment (MSP) to Rio Tinto equal to a percentage of
all capital costs and operating costs incurred by Oyu Tolgoi from March 31, 2010
onwards. After signing of the Underground Plan on May 18, 2015, the percentage 
applied
to capital costs of the underground development is 1.5%, and the percentage 
applied to operating costs and capital related to current operations is 3%. 
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-
bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:7pt" 
BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(iv)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:7pt">Rio Tinto recovers the 
costs of providing general corporate support services and mine management 
services to Turquoise
Hill. Mine management services are provided by Rio Tinto in its capacity as the 
manager of Oyu Tolgoi. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-
top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:7pt" 
BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(v)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:7pt">As part of the project 
finance agreements, Rio Tinto agreed to provide a guarantee, known as the 
completion support
undertaking (&#147;CSU&#148;) in favour of the Commercial Banks and the Export 
Credit Agencies. In consideration for providing the CSU, Oyu Tolgoi and 
Turquoise Hill are required to pay Rio Tinto&nbsp;a fee equal to 2.5% of the 
amounts drawn under
the facility, of which 1.9% is payable by Oyu Tolgoi and 0.6% is payable by 
Turquoise Hill. The annual completion support fee of 2.5% on amounts drawn under
the facility is accounted for as a borrowing cost and included within interest 
expense and
similar charges. The fee is settled net of a benefit arising on amounts 
deposited with 9539549 Canada Inc. under the Cash Management Services Agreement 
described in (ii) above. The fee payment obligation will terminate on the date 
Rio Tinto&#146;s
CSU obligations to the project lenders terminate. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:ARIAL"><B>13.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;NON-GAAP MEASURES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify">The Company presents and refers to the following measures (non-
GAAP measures) which are not defined in IFRS. A description and calculation of 
these
measures is given below, and may differ from equivalent measures provided by 
other issuers. These measures are presented in order to provide investors and 
other stakeholders with a greater understanding of performance and operations at
Oyu Tolgoi.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:ARIAL"><B>Operating cash costs </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">The measure of 
operating cash costs
excludes: depreciation and depletion; exploration and evaluation; charges for 
asset write-down (including write-down of materials and supplies inventory), and
includes management services payments to Rio Tinto, and management services 
payments to
Turquoise Hill which are eliminated in the consolidated financial statements of 
the Company. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:ARIAL"><B>C1 cash costs </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify">C1 cash costs is a metric representing the cash cost per unit of
extracting and processing the Company&#146;s principal metal product to a 
condition in
which it may be delivered to customers, net of gold and silver credits 
from&nbsp;concentrates sold. It is provided in order to support peer group 
comparability and to provide investors and other stakeholders with useful 
information about the
underlying cash costs of Oyu Tolgoi and the impact of gold and silver credits on
the operations&#146; cost structure. C1 cash costs are relevant to understanding
the Company&#146;s operating profitability and ability to generate cash flow. 
When
calculating costs associated with producing a pound of copper, the Company 
includes gold and silver revenue credits as the production cost is reduced as a 
result of selling these products. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-
COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" ALIGN="center">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="51%"></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" WIDTH="2%"></TD>
<TD WIDTH="47%"></TD></TR>

STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-
size:8pt">June 30, 2016</P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" STYLE="BORDER-TOP:1px solid #000000">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>

&nbsp;15&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD></TR></TABLE>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:ARIAL"><B>Turquoise Hill Resources Ltd. </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-
family:ARIAL">Management&#146;s Discussion and Analysis of Financial Condition 
and Results of Operations </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:7pt; font-
family:ARIAL">(Stated in U.S. dollars, except where noted) </P> <P STYLE="line-
height:1.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1.00pt solid 
#000000">&nbsp;</P>
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"
ALIGN="justify">Turquoise Hill&#146;s principal metal product is copper and C1 
cash costs are reported for Oyu Tolgoi
only. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:ARIAL"><B>All-in sustaining costs </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">All-in 
sustaining costs
(AISC) is an extended cash based cost metric, providing further information on 
the aggregate cash, capital and overhead outlay per unit, and is intended to
reflect the costs of producing the Company&#146;s principal metal product in 
both the short
term and over the life-cycle of its operations; as a result, sustaining capital 
expenditure on a cash basis is included rather than depreciation. As the measure
seeks to present a full cost of copper production associated with sustaining 
current
operations, development project capital is not included. AISC allows Turquoise 
Hill to assess the ability of Oyu Tolgoi to support sustaining capital 
expenditures for future production from the generation of operating cash flows. 
</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" 
ALIGN="justify">A reconciliation of total operating cash costs, C1 cash costs 
and all-in sustaining costs is provided below. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:8pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
